Well, this is a diamond in the rough. <rate>5</rate><Review>This location is in an outdoor mall so has been getting extra merchandise while indoor malls have been closed. This store extended the semi annual summer sale because of that and I was able to get summer scents I liked at great prices while looking at new fall scents. They have set aside one hour a week for early shopping for more vulnerable shoppers. Check the store hours for more information. Weekday mornings have less shoppers. It is a small shop but set up well for getting around inside. I noticed it started to get kind of full closer to noon. Advise going early. Asked how to smell the scents and was told that it will be okay to quickly pull down face mask just to nose and then put back up. Touching the scent will fingers is strictly not allowed, nor touching caps with fingers or nose. I would advise not shopping in person if you are not comfortable with others smelling scents. Opt to order on line. I checked and the return policy is still in effect and you do have the option to return in store in ordering on line. I really need to be able to smell the scents to decide so I went ahead with pulling the mask down from nose, but didn't feel right or good about it. I limited myself to three scents to choose from and went away from other shoppers to smell them. I bought two of them.  Employees are all wearing masks. Distancing markers are at the registers. Plexiglass at the counter. There are limits to how many customers allowed in the store at one time and I have seen lines outside. The lines may get longer during the holiday season. <Rating>5</Rating>< review>
Good Concept, Decent Food
We had lunch at the La Canada branch of this fresh Mediterranean fast casual concept. Although somewhat Americanized, the ingredients were fresh and the food was fine. After ordering at the counter, the food is brought to your table as it is made (not necessarily all at once). The main difference between this place and more traditional places serving similar food is that Luna Grill is more expensive and has less bold flavors. The casual vibe was good for the kids and the staff was friendly and helpful.</review>

< text>
Chicken is very tasty.  I ordered a seasonal beet salad and added chicken. This is an order at the counter before being seated casual place.  Indo find their combinations a bit odd.  My salad had roasted tomatoes but fairly pedestrian  beets that could have come out of a can, which I love but I guess was expecting something a bit more elevated.  They serve hummus which I am not a big  fan of and do not serve baba ganoush/mouttabal (which I love!).   I tasted my lunch partner's.  It had a strange sweetness and was not that thick.  I realise there are many different cultures represented in Middle-Eastern cooking. Having never eaten at a Halal establishment and my expectations being based on my 50 or so years of  eating Israeli, Persian, Lebanese, and Armenian food probably coloured my perception but all-in-all food was fresh and tasty.  This is a good casual dining option in LA Canada.<//text>

< Review>
Living in town, I usually go to Ryderz about once a month.

It's usually never crowded so being seated and ordering is easy. The wait staff is friendly and will always take the time to get your order right.

The food is pretty average. Tasty, but nothing special. The portions are not always that generous.

The menu has a good number of choices. That is one of the things I like most about Ryderz.</Review>
